				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Weinen, Klagen, Sorgen, Zagen, BWV 12 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>7 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1714 (Original)<br />1724 (Revised) (in G&#160;minor)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<tr>
<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>This cantata shows the problem between chorton and kammerton. The strings and the organ was playing in chorton = ca 466 Hz (F minor) and the oboe (and probably the bassoon) in kammerton= 415Hz (G minor). I have made parts in both keys for you to choose.
</td></tr>

<tr>
<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>This cantata shows the problem between chorton and kammerton. The strings and the organ was playing in chorton = ca 466 Hz (F minor) and the oboe (and probably the bassoon) in kammerton= 415Hz (G minor). I have made parts in both keys for you to choose.
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Weinen, Klagen, Sorgen, Zagen
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Weeping, lamenting, worrying, fearing
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ca">Weinen</span>; <span title="he">Weinen, Klagen, Sorgen, Zagen, רי"ב 12</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/178291408">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Weinen,_Klagen,_Sorgen,_Zagen,_BWV_12">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/178291408">178291408</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300006888">300006888</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb139094759">139094759</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 12&#160;; BC A 68
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 694
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>F Dorian mode&#160;; rev. G&#160;minor
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>7 movements:
<ol><li> Sinfonia (F Dorian mode)
</li><li> Chorus (alto): Weinen, Klagen, Sorgen, Zagen (F Dorian mode)
</li><li> Recitative (alto): Wir müssen durch viel Trübsal (C&#160;minor)
</li><li> Aria (alto): Kreuz und Kronen sind verbunden (C&#160;minor)
</li><li> Aria (bass): Ich folge Christo nach (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li> Aria (alto): Sei getreu, alle Pein (G&#160;minor)
</li><li> Chorale: Was Gott tut, das ist wohlgetan (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1714 (Original)<br />1724 (Revised) (in G&#160;minor)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>

</td></tr>
